\subsubsection[{reduce}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}template$<$int N, typename T , class Op $>$ \-\_\-\-\_\-device\-\_\-\-\_\- \-\_\-\-\_\-forceinline\-\_\-\-\_\- {\bf void} cv\-::gpu\-::device\-::reduce (
